2026-03-28 01:14:00 - Saqib Uni: Karakoram International University (KIU), in collaboration with Friedrich-Alexander-Universität Erlangen-Nürnberg (FAU), Germany, invites applications for the Erasmus+ Mobility Program (SMS171), offering students a one-semester exchange opportunity in Germany.
The program is being implemented under the supervision of Dr. Aftab Ahmed Khan, Project Investigator. It is open to Master’s (2nd semester) students from the Departments of GIS/Remote Sensing, Environmental Sciences, and Geology & Mountain Hazards. Applicants should have a minimum CGPA of 3.0 and a strong motivation to gain international academic exposure.
🎓 Financial Support Includes:
• Travel Grant: €1,188
• Monthly Scholarship: €900
• Initial two months’ payment upon arrival
📑 Required Documents:
• Student ID
• Motivation Letter
• Academic Transcripts (BS & MS)
📧 Apply at: iok@kiu.edu.pk
📅 Deadline: March 31, 2026
This program provides an excellent opportunity for students to study at a leading European university, enhance research capabilities, and build international academic networks.

2026-04-01 19:02:00 - Sha g Uni: 📢 Attention all GB candidates:
🎓GILGIT-BALTISTAN EDUCATIONAL ENDOWMENT FUND SCHOLARSHIP 

⏰The deadline for submitting the online Application Form has been extended to April 5, 2026

📄 Submission of hard copies is not required. All necessary documents must be uploaded while completing the online application form.

📌Important Note:
-Students who have not completed the required data/ recent results as per policy will not be eligible for this scholarship.
-Incomplete form submissions will not be entertained.
-Forms submitted with incomplete information will not be considered

📢 Eligibility Criteria for Gilgit-Baltistan Educational Endowment Fund Scholarship: 
1. Have a Gilgit-Baltistan domicile.
2. Last passed annual examination (current result).
3. Passed these examinations through a Government institution.
4. Students nominated by the GB Directorate are also eligible.
5. Intermediate (HSSC-I & II) and DAE (I, II & III) in public sector colleges under the Higher Education Department, GB.
6. BS and ADP students in public sector colleges of GB.
7. Students from GB nominated through the Higher Education Department GB, who are enrolled in Intermediate, ADP, MBBS, BDS, DVM, Agriculture, Pharm-D, Law, Engineering, and general BS programs at recognized universities and institutions across Pakistan—including local colleges/universities of GB—as well as students admitted on a merit basis to reputed public sector universities/institutions, are eligible.
8. Minimum CGPA / Annual Exam Percentage requirements for scholarship:
Public Sector Universities/Colleges: ≥ 70% equivalent CGPA for Sciences and ≥ 70% equivalent CGPA for Arts
Public Sector Medical and Dental Colleges: ≥ 70% in annual exams (Selection of merit criteria)
9. The applicant must not be receiving any other scholarship during the current academic year.
🌐 Web Link for Online Nomination Application:



https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029Vb7ZMAz7j6g1CxpDXi06

، ہم، قراقرم انٹرنیشنل یونیورسٹی، گلگت بلتستان کے وہ طلبہ جو پنجاب حکومت کی جانب سے دی جانے والی ہونہار اسکالرشپ پر منتخب ہونے پر، پنجاب حکومت، بالخصوص محترمہ وزیراعلیٰ مریم نواز صاحبہ کے نہایت مشکور ہیں کہ انہوں نے یہ اسکالرشپ رکھی، لیکن نہایت افسوس کے ساتھ کہنا پڑ رہا ہے کہ یہ اسکالرشپ گزشتہ 10 سے 11 ماہ سے التواء کا شکار ہے۔
اس تاخیر کے باعث طلبہ کو درج ذیل سنگین مسائل کا سامنا ہے:
• لیٹ فیس چارجز لگنا
• ایل ایم ایس (Learning Management System) کی بندش
• فیس ادا نہ ہونے کی وجہ سے امتحانات میں شرکت سے محرومی
• دیگر اسکالرشپس کے لیے درخواست دینے سے محرومی
• تعلیمی کارکردگی اور ذہنی سکون پر منفی اثر

2026-04-14 19:45:00 - Saqib Uni: The District Zakat & Ushr Committee Gilgit has provided Rs. 300,000 as scholarship assistance for deserving students of Karakoram International University (KIU).

According to KIU’s Directorate of Public Relations, the cheque was handed over by Chairman Haji Iqbal Dar to Director Financial Aid Shahid Ahmed Shigri. The ceremony was also attended by Internal Auditor Mushtaq Hussain and the Chairman’s representative Zahid Iqbal.

On the occasion, Shahid Ahmed Shigri expressed gratitude to the Zakat Committee, stating that such financial support plays a vital role in helping needy students continue their education and promotes educational equity in society. He assured that the funds will be distributed among deserving students with full transparency.

Chairman Haji Iqbal Dar emphasized that Zakat funds are meant to support underprivileged segments of society, and investing in education yields long-term positive outcomes. He reaffirmed the committee’s commitment to continue supporting KIU students in the future.

Both KIU’s Financial Aid Office and the District Zakat Committee agreed to further strengthen their collaboration to ensure that maximum deserving students benefit from such initiatives and continue their education without financial barriers.

2026-05-13 15:06:00 - +92 355 5106735: Here are the answers to all 15 MCQs:

1. **JNZ** — Jump if Zero Flag is not set
2. **SS** — BP register uses Stack Segment by default
3. **Register** — Uses registers only, no memory access
4. **SI and DI** — These hold offset address in indexed relative mode
5. **SI, DI, and BX** — Common pointers in register indirect mode
6. **67H** — 38H + 2FH = 67H
7. **MOV** — MOV has no effect on flag register
8. **CF** — Carry Flag is set on carry beyond MSB
9. **ZF** — Zero Flag becomes 1 when result is zero
10. **BX and BP** — Used as base registers in based relative mode
11. **DS** — Default segment register for MOV AL,[BX]
12. **18638H** — Physical = DS×16 + offset = 15120H + 3518H = 18638H
13. **Based indexed** — Combines one base + one index register
14. **7** — 80x86 has 7 addressing modes
15. **A constant value** — Source operand is a constant in immediate mode

2026-06-01 18:25:00 - Saqib Uni: SDGs (Sustainable Development Goals) 17 goals hain jo United Nations ne 2015 mein banaye. In ka maqsad duniya ko behtar banana hai taake logon ko achi zindagi mil sake, ghurbat kam ho, aur environment mehfooz rahe.

2026-06-01 18:26:00 - +92 346 7445686: G yah to Samaj aaya hai but project ma ppts bana ky present krna hai kia?

2026-06-01 18:26:00 - Saqib Uni: 17 SDGs aur Unki Simple Explanation
No Poverty – Ghurbat khatam karna.
Zero Hunger – Sab ko kafi aur sehatmand khana milna.
Good Health and Well-being – Sab ki sehat aur khushhali behtar banana.
Quality Education – Har shakhs ko achi taleem dena.
Gender Equality – Mardon aur aurton ko barabar huqooq dena.
Clean Water and Sanitation – Saaf pani aur safai ki sahulat dena.
Affordable and Clean Energy – Sasti aur saaf energy muhayya karna.
Decent Work and Economic Growth – Rozgar aur maashi taraqqi ko barhana.
Industry, Innovation and Infrastructure – Technology, industries aur infrastructure ko behtar banana.
Reduced Inequalities – Logon ke darmiyan na-insafi aur farq kam karna.
Sustainable Cities and Communities – Shehron ko mehfooz aur behtar banana.
Responsible Consumption and Production – Wasail ka zimmeydari se istemal karna.
Climate Action – Climate change ke khilaf qadam uthana.
Life Below Water – Samandari zindagi ki hifazat karna.
Life on Land – Jungle, janwar aur zameeni mahol ki hifazat karna.
Peace, Justice and Strong Institutions – Aman, insaf aur mazboot idaray banana.
Partnerships for the Goals – Mulkon aur organizations ka mil kar kaam karna.

2026-06-22 16:02:00 - Saqib Uni: Here are the exact correct answers for all 15 questions, with brief reasoning:

---

1. Which data structure allows dynamic memory allocation?
✅ Linked List
(Arrays are static; linked lists grow/shrink dynamically.)

2. Which register points to the top of the stack?
✅ SP (Stack Pointer)

3. Which flag is mainly checked after a CMP instruction?
✅ Zero Flag
(CMP subtracts operands; ZF is used for equality checks via JE/JNE.)

4. Which instruction jumps if the Zero Flag is set?
✅ JE (Jump if Equal)

5. Which instruction jumps if Carry Flag is set?
✅ JC (Jump if Carry)

6. LOOP continues execution while:
✅ CX ≠ 0
(LOOP decrements CX and jumps if CX is not zero.)

7. Which instruction is often used with loops for comparisons?
✅ CMP (Compare)

8. Which register is usually used as a loop counter?
✅ CX

9. Which register is commonly used as an index for arrays?
✅ SI (Source Index)

10. LOOP instruction automatically decrements which register?
✅ CX

11. Which instruction jumps if Carry Flag is not set?
✅ JNC (Jump if No Carry)

12. Which instruction can load an array element into a register?
✅ MOV (e.g., MOV AL, [SI])

13. Which instruction is commonly used for looping in Assembly?
✅ LOOP

14. Which register is commonly used to access array elements?
✅ SI (again)

15. What happens when CX becomes zero?
✅ Loop terminates
(Execution falls through to the next instruction after the loop.)

---

All answers are 100% accurate for standard x86/8086 Assembly. Ready for the next set!
